<script>
$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});
</script>

				<div class="page">
<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 0, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 0;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

			$(function(){
				var nLength = $('.slideList li').length;
				for(var i=0; i<$('.slideList li').length; i++){
					if(i%6==4){
						$('.slideList li').eq(i).after('<li class="line"></li>');
						i+=2
					}
				}
				if((nLength-1)%5!=4){

$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 1, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 1;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 2, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 2;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 3, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 3;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择

       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');

       };

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 4, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 4;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script>
$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 5, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 5;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

				<div class="page">
<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 6, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 6;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 7, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 7;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 8, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 8;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

			$(function(){
				var nLength = $('.slideList li').length;
				for(var i=0; i<$('.slideList li').length; i++){
					if(i%6==4){
						$('.slideList li').eq(i).after('<li class="line"></li>');
						i+=2
					}
				}
				if((nLength-1)%5!=4){
					$('.slideList li:last').after('<li class="line"></li>');
				}
			});

<script>
$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});
</script>

				<div class="page">
<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 9, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 9;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script>
$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});
</script>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 10, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 10;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script>
$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 11, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 11;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;

       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){

       };

    if (fsy){

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 12, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 12;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 13, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 13;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

     var menuLeft=[];

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 14, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 14;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 15, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 15;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

				<div class="page">
<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 16, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 16;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>
			</div>
		</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 17, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 17;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

				<div class="page">
<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 18, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 18;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script>
$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});
</script>

				<div class="page">
<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 19, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 19;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

			$(function(){
				var nLength = $('.slideList li').length;
				for(var i=0; i<$('.slideList li').length; i++){
					if(i%6==4){
						$('.slideList li').eq(i).after('<li class="line"></li>');

					}
				}
				if((nLength-1)%5!=4){

     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});
</script>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 20, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 20;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 21, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 21;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script>
$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 22, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 22;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 23, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 23;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>

<script>
$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 24, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 24;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

				<div class="page">
<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 25, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 25;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>
			</div>
		</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 26, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 26;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];

     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){

       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');

	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");

});

				<div class="page">
<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 27, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 27;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 28, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 28;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 29, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 29;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script>
$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});
</script>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 30, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 30;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script>
$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 31, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 31;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 32, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 32;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>

     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

					var currentPage = 33;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>
			</div>
		</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 34, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 34;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 35, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 35;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

			$(function(){
				var nLength = $('.slideList li').length;
				for(var i=0; i<$('.slideList li').length; i++){
					if(i%6==4){
						$('.slideList li').eq(i).after('<li class="line"></li>');
						i+=2
					}
				}
				if((nLength-1)%5!=4){
					$('.slideList li:last').after('<li class="line"></li>');
				}
			});

$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 36, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 36;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

     var fsy=true;

       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');

       };

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 37, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 37;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 38, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 38;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script>
$(function(){
     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});
</script>
