<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 39, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 39;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 40, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 40;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');

	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 41, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 41;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

					//createPageHTML(50, 42, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 42;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页

					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>
			</div>
		</div>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 43, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 43;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 44, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 44;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>

				}
				if((nLength-1)%5!=4){
					$('.slideList li:last').after('<li class="line"></li>');
				}
			});
		</script>
	</body>

$(function(){

     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择

       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");
    }

});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 45, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 45;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

	       fsy=false;
       };

    if (fsy){

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 46, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 46;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 47, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 47;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

     var checkelement=window.location.href;
     var menu=[];
     var menuLeft=[];
     var length=$(".topNavBox li").length;
     var fsy=true;
	 //头部当前页选择
　　 for (i=0;i<length;i++){
       menu.push($(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').attr("href"));
       if(checkelement.indexOf(menu[i])>=0){
               $(".topNavBox li a").removeClass('on');
	       $(".topNavBox li").eq(i).children('a').addClass('on');
	       fsy=false;
       };
　　};
    if (fsy){
	    $(".topNavBox li:first").addClass("on");

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 48, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 48;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>

     var fsy=true;

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/JavaScript">
					//createPageHTML(50, 49, "index", "shtml");
					var currentPage = 49;//所在页从0开始
					//var headPage = "index"+"."+"shtml";//首页
					//var tailPage = "index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml"//尾页
					var prevPage = currentPage-1//上一页
					var nextPage = currentPage+1//下一页
					var countPage = 50//共多少页
					

					document.write("<span class='total'>共"+countPage+"页</span>");
					//设置上一页代码
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage!=1)
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index"+"_" + prevPage + "."+"shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=0&&currentPage==1)
					
						document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\">首页</a><a href=\"index.shtml\">上一页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>首页</span><span class='back'>上一页</span>");
					//循环
					var num = 5;
					for(var i=0+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num) ; i<=(num+(currentPage-1-(currentPage-1)%num))&&(i<countPage) ; i++){
						if(currentPage==i)
							document.write("<span class='on'>"+(i+1)+"</span>");
						else if(i==0){
							document.write("<a href=\"index.shtml\" class='num'>"+1+"</a>");
						}else 
							document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + i + "."+"shtml\" class='num'>"+(i+1)+"</a>");
					}
					
					//设置下一页代码 
					if(countPage>1&&currentPage!=(countPage-1))
						document.write("<a href=\"index"+"_" + nextPage + "."+"shtml\" class='back'>下一页</a><a class='back' href=\"index_" + (countPage-1) + ".shtml\">尾页</a>");
					else
						document.write("<span class='back'>下一页</span><span class='back'>尾页</span>");
						
					</script>
</div>
			</div>
